             <img alt="barci-rafting" class="attachment-vw_medium size-vw_medium wp-post-image" data-attachment-id="3334" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="barci-rafting" data-large-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/barci-rafting-1024x683.jpg" data-medium-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/barci-rafting-550x367.jpg" data-orig-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/barci-rafting.jpg" data-orig-size="1200,800" data-permalink="http://hibiscussport.ro/barci-rafting/barci-rafting-2/" height="420" src="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/barci-rafting-750x420.jpg" width="750"/>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="post-box-inner">
            <h3 class="title">
             <a href="http://hibiscussport.ro/categorie-produs/rafting/" rel="bookmark" title="Barci rafting">
              Barci rafting
             </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="post-excerpt ">
             Bărcile, canoele și caiacele gonflabile pentru rafting sunt concepute pentru sportivii experimentați în coborârea râurilor repezi cu un grad mare de dificultate. Aceste bărci sunt robuste, durabile si sigure, vin echipate cu orificii de auto-drenare și numeroase elemente de siguranță.
            </div>
            <div class="post-box-footer clearfix">
             <a class="read-more" href="http://hibiscussport.ro/categorie-produs/rafting/" rel="bookmark" title="Barci rafting">
              Vezi produsele
              <i class="icon-entypo-right-open">
              </i>
             </a>
            </div>

           <div class="post-thumbnail-wrapper">
            <a href="http://hibiscussport.ro/categorie-produs/canoe/" rel="bookmark" title="Canoe">
             <img alt="Canoe" class="attachment-vw_medium size-vw_medium wp-post-image" data-attachment-id="2532" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="canoe" data-large-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/canoe-1024x683.jpg" data-medium-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/canoe-550x367.jpg" data-orig-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/canoe.jpg" data-orig-size="1200,800" data-permalink="http://hibiscussport.ro/canoe/canoe-2/" height="420" src="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/canoe-750x420.jpg" width="750"/>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="post-box-inner">
            <h3 class="title">
             <a href="http://hibiscussport.ro/categorie-produs/canoe/" rel="bookmark" title="Canoe">
              Canoe
             </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="post-excerpt ">
             Canoele pot fi folosite in excursii de agrement, ture de cateva zile sau in coborarea raurilor repezi de munte. Designul si  materialele de constructie difera in functie de utilizarea dorita. Oferta noastra cuprinde canoe Robson, Tahe Marine si Gumotex (gonlfabile).
             <br/>
            </div>
            <div class="post-box-footer clearfix">

           <div class="post-thumbnail-wrapper">
            <a href="http://hibiscussport.ro/categorie-produs/open-bic/" rel="bookmark" title="Open BIC">
             <img alt="" class="attachment-vw_medium size-vw_medium wp-post-image" data-attachment-id="27" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"1375435648","copyright":"Matias Capizzano","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"Photo: Matias Capizzano"}' data-image-title="Photo: Matias Capizzano" data-large-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/Open-BIC-1024x682.jpg" data-medium-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/Open-BIC-550x366.jpg" data-orig-file="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/Open-BIC.jpg" data-orig-size="1200,800" data-permalink="http://hibiscussport.ro/photo-matias-capizzano/" height="420" src="http://hibiscussport.ro/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/Open-BIC-750x420.jpg" width="750"/>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="post-box-inner">
            <h3 class="title">
             <a href="http://hibiscussport.ro/categorie-produs/open-bic/" rel="bookmark" title="Open BIC">
              Open BIC
             </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="post-excerpt ">
             Open BIC este o iola care face legatura intre Optimist si barcile cu vele pentru adulti.
             <br/>
             Se adreseaza in special copiilor si adolescentilor, desi constructia barcii permite oricui adult pana in 90 de kg sa navigheze cu aceasta ambarcatiune. Open BIC este clasa ISAF.
            </div>

             <a href="http://hibiscussport.ro/nou-java-caiac-sit-on-top-pentru-ture/" rel="bookmark" title="Nou: Java, caiac sit on top pentru ture">
              Nou: Java, caiac sit on top pentru ture
             </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="post-meta header-font">
             <img alt="" class="avatar avatar-32 photo" height="32" src="http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/b26bb08c4d305023841cd770fdfcf55f?s=32&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/b26bb08c4d305023841cd770fdfcf55f?s=64&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" width="32"/>

              Hibiscus Sport
             </a>

             <a class="post-date" href="http://hibiscussport.ro/nou-java-caiac-sit-on-top-pentru-ture/" rel="bookmark" title="Nou: Java, caiac sit on top pentru ture">
              3 februarie 2017
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="post-excerpt ">
             <p>
              Mult-așteptatul caiac Java este acum disponibil ! Mai lung, mai rapid și mai stabil decât legendarul Bilbao, cu un spațiu generos pentru bagaje la bord Java este un caiac …
             </p>
